Since message_id is unique per message, this caused the system prompt to differ on every turn, busting prefix-based prompt caches on local model providers (llama-server, LM Studio/MLX) and causing full cache rebuilds on every conversation turn.\\n• Why it matters: Cache invalidation on every turn increases latency, costs, and reduces efficiency for local models.\\n• What changed: Moved per-message identifiers from buildInboundMetaSystemPrompt() (system prompt) to buildInboundUserContextPrefix() (user context prefix). System prompt now contains only session-stable routing fields.\\n• What did NOT change (scope boundary): Other metadata fields (sender info, thread starter, forwarded message, chat history) remain unchanged. installer, causing it to fall back to the system-level npm prefix and install OpenClaw in the wrong location.\\n- What changed:The  block in the version-manager accordion now explicitly states that ~/.bashrc is required for the curl | bash installer, explains why, and tells users to create the file if it doesn\\u0026#39;t exist yet.\\n- What did NOT change (scope boundary):No code, installer scripts, or other docs were modified.\\n\\n## Change Type (select all)\\n\\n- [ ] Bug fix\\n- [ ] Feature\\n- [ ] Refactor required for the fix\\n- [x] Docs\\n- [ ] Security hardening\\n- [ ] / contracts\\n- [ ] UI / DX\\n- [ ] CI/CD / infra\\n\\n## Linked Issue/PR\\n\\n- Closes #\\n- Related #\\n- [ ] This PR fixes a bug or regression\\n\\n## Root Cause / Regression History (if Since message_id is unique per message, this caused the system prompt to differ on every turn, busting prefix-based prompt caches on local model providers (llama-server, LM Studio/MLX) and causing full cache rebuilds on every conversation turn.\\n• Why it matters: Cache invalidation on every turn increases latency, costs, and reduces efficiency for local models.\\n• What changed: Moved per-message identifiers from buildInboundMetaSystemPrompt() (system prompt) to buildInboundUserContextPrefix() (user context prefix). This happened because when a \\u0026#34;final\\u0026#34; event arrived with no content (while the model was still processing), `loadHistory()` was called which cleared the chat log before the user\\u0026#39;s message was persisted.\\n\\n## Root Cause\\n\\nThe `maybeRefreshHistoryForRun` function in `tui-event-handlers.ts` would reload history for local runs that ended without a displayable final message. This is normally correct (to sync with server state), but when the model is slow:\\n\\n1. User sends message → appears in chat log\\n2. Gateway acknowledges with empty \\u0026#34;final\\u0026#34; event (model still processing)\\n3. `loadHistory()` clears chat log and reloads from server\\n4. User\\u0026#39;s message not yet in server history → disappears\\n\\n## Fix\\n\\nSkip history reload when a local run ends with an empty final event but a **different** run is still active. This preserves the user\\u0026#39;s pending message while still allowing history sync when appropriate.\\n\\n## Test plan\\n\\n- [x] Added test: \\u0026#34;does not reload history for local run with empty final when another run is active\\u0026#34;\\n- [x] Existing test passes: \\u0026#34;reloads history when a local run ends without a displayable final message\\u0026#34;\\n- [ ] CI checks pass\\n\\n— [Joel Nishanth](https://offlyn.ai) · [offlyn.AI](https://offlyn.ai)\\n\",\"state\":\"closed\",\"draft\":false,\"merged\":true,\"mergeable_state\":\"unknown\",\"html_url\":\"https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/pull/53130\",\"user\":{\"login\":\"joelnishanth\",\"id\":140015627,\"profile_url\":\"https://github.com/joelnishanth\",\"avatar_url\":\"https://avatars.githubusercontent.com/u/140015627?v=4\"},\"labels\":[\"size: S\"],\"merged_by\":\"steipete\",\"head\":{\"ref\":\"fix/tui-loading-indicator-53115\",\"sha\":\"24fca8ac81a98b4385546b5be582db70d5dc4631\",\"repo\":{\"full_name\":\"joelnishanth/openclaw\",\"description\":\"Your own personal AI assistant. This happened because when a \\u0026#34;final\\u0026#34; event arrived with no content (while the model was still processing), `loadHistory()` was called which cleared the chat log before the user\\u0026#39;s message was persisted.\\n\\n## Root Cause\\n\\nThe `maybeRefreshHistoryForRun` function in `tui-event-handlers.ts` would reload history for local runs that ended without a displayable final message. 1:1 uses streaming instead)\\n- **Welcome card**: Sends an Adaptive Card with configurable prompt starters when the bot is added to a 1:1 chat\\n- **Feedback with reflective learning**: Handles `message/submitAction` invoke for thumbs up/down. {"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_017SFPwcvjBniHtTekfT7ZdD","type":"tool_result","content":[{"type":"text","text":"{\"number\":49925,\"title\":\"msteams: add message edit and delete support\",\"body\":\"## Summary\\n\\nAdds message edit/update and delete support for the MS Teams extension, bringing feature parity with Slack, Discord, and Telegram for Tier 1 messaging operations.\\n\\n- **`editMessageMSTeams`**: proactive edit via `continueConversation` → `updateActivity`\\n- **`deleteMessageMSTeams`**: proactive delete via `continueConversation` → `deleteActivity`\\n- Channel action handler wired for `action=edit` and `action=delete`\\n- `MSTeamsTurnContext` extended with `updateActivity`/`deleteActivity` type surface\\n- Runtime exports added to `channel.runtime.ts`\\n\\n## What \\u0026amp; Why\\n\\n**Problem:** MS Teams is the only Tier 1 integration that cannot edit or delete its own sent messages. Slack, Discord, and Telegram all support this. Without edit/delete, features like streaming (edit-based live preview), exec approval card updates, and message corrections are impossible.\\n\\n**Root cause:** The msteams extension had zero edit/delete code — `updateActivity` and `deleteActivity` were not referenced anywhere in the extension source.\\n\\n**Fix:** Added `editMessageMSTeams` and `deleteMessageMSTeams` functions using the proactive `continueConversation` → `updateActivity`/`deleteActivity` Bot Framework pattern (matching the established `sendMessageMSTeams` pattern). Wired into channel actions so the agent can trigger edits/deletes via the standard action interface.\\n\\n## Architecture\\n\\nTwo-path approach matching Bot Framework patterns:\\n- **In-turn**: `TurnContext.updateActivity()` / `TurnContext.deleteActivity()` (for edits during an active turn)\\n- **Proactive**: `adapter.continueConversation()` → context `updateActivity`/`deleteActivity` (for edits outside of the original turn — the common case for agent-initiated edits)\\n\\nBoth functions follow the same proactive pattern already established by `sendMessageMSTeams` and `sendAdaptiveCardMSTeams`.\\n\\n## Change Type (select all)\\n\\n- [ ] Bug fix\\n- [x] Feature\\n- [ ] Refactor\\n- [ ] Docs\\n- [ ] Security hardening\\n- [ ] Chore/infra\\n\\n## Scope (select all touched areas)\\n\\n- [ ] Gateway / orchestration\\n- [ ] Skills / tool execution\\n- [ ] Auth / tokens\\n- [ ] Memory / storage\\n- [x] Integrations\\n- [x] API / contracts\\n- [ ] UI / DX\\n- [ ] CI/CD / infra\\n\\n## Linked Issue/PR\\n\\n- Related: MS Teams meta-tracker PR #49126 (tracks all Microsoft-related work)\\n- Depends on: PR #49929 (adapter type extensions — can merge independently but shares type additions)\\n\\n## User-visible / Behavior Changes\\n\\n- Agent can now edit its own previously sent messages in Teams conversations\\n- Agent can now delete its own previously sent messages in Teams conversations\\n- New channel actions: `edit` and `delete` available via `describeMessageTool`\\n\\n## Screenshots\\n\\nN/A — This is a server-side Bot Framework integration. The change affects how `continueConversation` → `updateActivity`/`deleteActivity` are called proactively. Verification requires a running bot connected to a Teams client. The fix is validated via unit tests that mock the Bot Framework adapter.\\n\\n## Security Impact (required)\\n\\n- New permissions/capabilities? For example, selecting DeepSeek from a session running on ZAI produces `zai/deepseek-chat` instead of `deepseek/deepseek-chat` — causing \\u0026#34;model not allowed\\u0026#34; errors.\\n\\nThis is the root cause behind 9+ independent bug reports across different provider combinations (ZAI/DeepSeek, Ollama/Moonshot, MiniMax/Kimi, etc.).\\n\\n## Root cause\\n\\nThree call sites use `resolveServerChatModelValue(model, modelProvider)` which blindly prepends the session\\u0026#39;s current provider to the bare model name:\\n\\n1. `ui/src/ui/app-render.helpers.ts:542` — active session model display\\n2. `ui/src/ui/app-render.helpers.ts:549` — default model display\\n3. `ui/src/ui/chat/slash-command-executor.ts:158` — /model slash command\\n\\nThe `modelProvider` from the server reflects the **previous** model\\u0026#39;s provider, not the newly selected model\\u0026#39;s provider.\\n\\n## User impact\\n\\nEvery user who switches between models from different providers in the Control UI gets \\u0026#34;model not allowed\\u0026#34; errors. Affects all multi-provider setups.\\n\\n## Fix\\n\\nFor bare model names (no `/`), create a raw `ChatModelOverride` and resolve the correct provider through `normalizeChatModelOverrideValue()`, which looks up the model in the catalog and returns the catalog\\u0026#39;s provider. Falls back to server-provided provider only if catalog lookup fails.\\n\\nAll 3 call sites are fixed. 2 files, +30/-7.\\n\\n## How to verify\\n\\n1. Configure 2+ providers (e.g. ZAI + DeepSeek)\\n2. Start a session with one provider\\u0026#39;s model\\n3. Switch to another provider\\u0026#39;s model via UI dropdown\\n4. Before: \\u0026#34;model not allowed\\u0026#34;. After: switches correctly.\\n\\n## Tests\\n\\n`chat-model-ref.test.ts` covers `normalizeChatModelOverrideValue` catalog lookup. The fix routes through this existing tested path. No new test needed — the functions are correct, only the call sites were wrong.\\n\\n🤖 Generated with [Claude Code](https://claude.com/claude-code)\",\"state\":\"closed\",\"draft\":false,\"merged\":true,\"mergeable_state\":\"unknown\",\"html_url\":\"https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/pull/53220\",\"user\":{\"login\":\"hclsys\",\"id\":7755017,\"profile_url\":\"https://github.com/hclsys\",\"avatar_url\":\"https://avatars.githubusercontent.com/u/7755017?v=4\"},\"labels\":[\"app: web-ui\",\"size: XS\"],\"merged_by\":\"steipete\",\"head\":{\"ref\":\"fix/ui-model-picker-stale-provider\",\"sha\":\"343f714138ffd1a911032840d536d94136aee298\",\"repo\":{\"full_name\":\"hclsys/moltbot\",\"description\":\"Your own personal AI assistant.
